add an evhtp\-\_\-t structure (with its own callbacks) to a base evhtp\-\_\-t structure for virtual hosts. It should be noted that if you enable S\-S\-L on the base evhtp\-\_\-t and your version of Open\-S\-S\-L supports S\-N\-I, the S\-N\-I hostname will always take precedence over the Host header value.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}
add an evhtp\-\_\-t structure (with its own callbacks) to a base evhtp\-\_\-t structure for virtual hosts. It should be noted that if you enable S\-S\-L on the base evhtp\-\_\-t and your version of Open\-S\-S\-L supports S\-N\-I, the S\-N\-I hostname will always take precedence over the Host header value.

N\-O\-T\-E\-: If S\-S\-L is being used and the vhost was found via S\-N\-I, the Host\-: header will {\itshape N\-O\-T} be used to find a matching vhost.

Also, any hooks which are set prior to finding a vhost that are hooks which are after the host hook, they are overwritten by the callbacks and hooks set for the vhost specific evhtp\-\_\-t structure.

creates a new evhtp\-\_\-callback\-\_\-t structure. 

All callbacks are stored in this structure which define what the final function to be called after all parsing is done. A callback can be either a static string or a regular expression.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em path} & can either be a static path (/path/to/resource/) or a P\-O\-S\-I\-X compatible regular expression ($^\wedge$/resource/(.$\ast$)) \\
\hline
{\em type} & informs the function what type of of information is is contained within the path argument. This can either be callback\-\_\-type\-\_\-path, or callback\-\_\-type\-\_\-regex. \\
\hline
{\em cb} & the callback function to be invoked \\
\hline
{\em arg} & optional argument which is passed when the callback is executed.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on error.

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\item[{const char $\ast$}]{needle}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{evhtp_8h_a29fc979de78d3f9f671d0aaa593a7161}


attempts to find the callback matching the exact string 'needle'. This is useful in cases where we want to get the original handle, but is not in scope. 

with pattern based callbacks, this does not attempt to find a callback that would match the string if the pattern matcher was executed.

Meaning\-: evhtp\-\_\-set\-\_\-glob\-\_\-cb(htp, \char`\"{}/foo/bar$\ast$\char`\"{}, ....);

Calling evhtp\-\_\-get\-\_\-cb(htp, \char`\"{}/foo/bar/baz\char`\"{});

Will return N\-U\-L\-L since it's not the exact pattern set

Calling evhtp\-\_\-get\-\_\-cb(htp, \char`\"{}/foo/bar$\ast$\char`\"{});

Is the correct usage.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em htp} & \\
\hline
{\em needle} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
N\-U\-L\-L if callback is not not found 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Definition at line 3674 of file evhtp.\-c.

\hypertarget{evhtp_8h_a77933df4d525c46ca185ac424892a824}{\index{evhtp.\-h@{evhtp.\-h}!evhtp\-\_\-set\-\_\-hook@{evhtp\-\_\-set\-\_\-hook}}
\index{evhtp\-\_\-set\-\_\-hook@{evhtp\-\_\-set\-\_\-hook}!evhtp.h@{evhtp.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{evhtp\-\_\-set\-\_\-hook}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\-V\-H\-T\-P\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T int evhtp\-\_\-set\-\_\-hook (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf evhtp\-\_\-hooks\-\_\-t} $\ast$$\ast$}]{hooks, }
\item[{{\bf evhtp\-\_\-hook\-\_\-type}}]{type, }
\item[{{\bf evhtp\-\_\-hook}}]{cb, }
\item[{void $\ast$}]{arg}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{evhtp_8h_a77933df4d525c46ca185ac424892a824}


sets a callback hook for either a connection or a path/regex . 

A user may set a variety of hooks either per-\/connection, or per-\/callback. This allows the developer to hook into various parts of the request processing cycle.

a per-\/connection hook can be set at any time, but it is recommended to set these during either a pre-\/accept phase, or post-\/accept phase. This allows a developer to set hooks before any other hooks are called.

a per-\/callback hook works differently. In this mode a developer can setup a set of hooks prior to starting the event loop for specific callbacks. For example if you wanted to hook something O\-N\-L\-Y for a callback set by evhtp\-\_\-set\-\_\-cb or evhtp\-\_\-set\-\_\-regex\-\_\-cb this is the method of doing so.

per-\/callback example\-:

evhtp\-\_\-callback\-\_\-t $\ast$ cb = evhtp\-\_\-set\-\_\-regex\-\_\-cb(htp, \char`\"{}/anything/(.$\ast$)\char`\"{}, default\-\_\-cb, N\-U\-L\-L);

evhtp\-\_\-set\-\_\-hook(\&cb-\/$>$hooks, evhtp\-\_\-hook\-\_\-on\-\_\-headers, anything\-\_\-headers\-\_\-cb, N\-U\-L\-L);

evhtp\-\_\-set\-\_\-hook(\&cb-\/$>$hooks, evhtp\-\_\-hook\-\_\-on\-\_\-fini, anything\-\_\-fini\-\_\-cb, N\-U\-L\-L);

With the above example, once libevhtp has determined that it has a user-\/defined callback for /anything/.$\ast$; anything\-\_\-headers\-\_\-cb will be executed after all headers have been parsed, and anything\-\_\-fini\-\_\-cb will be executed before the request is free()'d.

The same logic applies to per-\/connection hooks, but it should be noted that if a per-\/callback hook is set, the per-\/connection hook will be ignored.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em hooks} & double pointer to the evhtp\-\_\-hooks\-\_\-t structure \\
\hline
{\em type} & the hook type \\
\hline
{\em cb} & the callback to be executed. \\
\hline
{\em arg} & optional argument which is passed when the callback is executed\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on error (if hooks is N\-U\-L\-L, it is allocated) 
\end{DoxyReturn}
